‚ö°Ô∏èüá∑üá∫ Kremlin: Sanctions against Russia are like a boomerang, returning to the Europeans; Putin participates in the G20 summit

Commenting on the text of the "Observer" newspaper, which states that the ban on the import of diamonds from Russia as part of the upcoming 12th package of EU sanctions will affect jewelry containing diamonds and pearls, Kremlin spokesman Dmitry Peskov says that this is just a continuation of the search for sanctions that could hit Russia anyway.

But, as a rule, the boomerang effect works. The interests of the Europeans themselves suffer. So far, we have managed to find ways to minimize the negative consequences of sanctions

Peskov points out.

The Kremlin spokesman confirmed that Russian President Vladimir Putin will participate in the G20 virtual summit hosted by India on November 22.
